H~ow~ a~re~ y~ou~?（伴隨著斷斷續續的雜音模仿）」外國朋友愣了一下，疑惑地問：「Excuse me? Are you... OK? Your voice sounds like a broken radio.」他得意地回答：「Yes! I learned English from the radio! It’s very good, right?
